reachbreaker_101 = {

	3296.10.19 = { 
		birth = yes

			add_character_flag = has_scripted_appearance
		}
	}
	3326.1.1 = { add_spouse = woodhewn_98_sister }
	3350.1.1 = {
		effect = {	
			if = {
				limit = { character:reachbreaker_105 = { is_alive = yes } }
				set_relation_rival = { reason = rival_historical target = character:reachbreaker_105 }
			}
		}
	}
	3351.9.7 = {
		effect = {
			add_gold = 200
		}
	}
	3354.1.1 = {
		effect = {
			add_opinion = {
				modifier = betrayed_me_opinion
				target = character:cursebraid_1000 # Svartr didn't help against reachfolk
				opinion = -50
			}
		}
	}
	3362.1.1 = { death = { death_reason = death_burned killer = reachbreaker_105 } } #Killed by Reachfolk along the rest of the family
}

	trait = cynical
	trait = humble

		effect = {
			if = { #This is how a minor house got his family into the Whiterun line
				limit = { character:yngvlar_2000_brother = { is_alive = yes } }
				set_relation_best_friend = { reason = friend_generic_history target = character:yngvlar_2000_brother }
			}
		}
	}
	#Marries Wulfmare Honeymaw in 3363.8.13, starts betrothed in 440
	3362.4.26 = { add_trait = depressed_1 } #Beloved brother dies
	3408.7.19 = { death = { death_reason = death_old_age } }
}

hodgrym_99 = {
	name = "Iona" #Duke of Greymarch
	dna = hodgrym_iona_dna_entry
	female = yes
	dynasty = 310006
	culture = westmarcher
	religion = nord_cult
	father = yngvlar_995
	mother = kjarnesen_103

	trait = calm
	trait = stubborn
	trait = deceitful
	trait = sign_apprentice

	trait = curious

	disallow_random_traits = yes

	3345.7.14 = { birth = yes }
	3355.5.7 = { set_relation_friend = { reason = friend_children_stole_alcohol target = character:twicestabbed_100 } }
	3358.4.3 = {
		effect = {
			if = {
				limit = { is_married = no }
				create_betrothal_matrilineal = character:twicestabbed_100
			}
		}
	}
	3361.7.14 = {
		add_trait = education_stewardship_2
		remove_trait = curious
	}
	3364.9.5 = { add_matrilineal_spouse = twicestabbed_100 }
	3365.5.11 = { dynasty_house = yngvlar_hodgrym } #This is to make her children not be displayed oddly
	3410.4.6 = { death = { death_reason = death_old_age } }
	portrait_override={
		portrait_modifier_overrides={
			custom_beards=female_empty
			custom_hair=female_hair_fp1_01
		}
	}
}

	}

lothid_101 = { 
	name = "Freyleth"
	dynasty = lothid
	religion = nord_cult
	culture = eastmarcher
	female = yes
	father = lothid_100 #probably not but why not
	
	trait = ambitious #took over her clan
	trait = callous #killed many innocent to achieve her goal
	trait = deceitful #lied to her closest relations to get ahead
	trait = schemer #see above
	trait = education_intrigue_4
	
	3280.1.1 = { birth = yes }
	3300.1.1 = { 
		trait = vampire_character
		effect = { 
			set_immortal_age = 20
			if = {
				limit = { character:ravenn_1001 = { is_alive = yes } }
				set_relation_rival = { reason = rival_historical target = character:ravenn_1001 }
			}
			if = {
				limit = { character:lothid_100 = { is_alive = yes } }
				set_relation_rival = { reason = rival_historical target = character:lothid_100 }
			}
		} 
	}
	3360.1.1 = { employer = lothid_100 }
	3504.1.1 = { death = yes }
}

	religion = nord_cult
	culture = eastmarcher
	
	trait = education_magic_3
	trait = education_learning_3
	trait = sign_mage
	
	learning = 11
	
	3200.4.1 = {
		birth = yes
		effect = { #for error purposes, perks gotta be given like this
			add_conjuration_perk_effect = { LEVEL = 4 }
			add_destruction_perk_effect = { LEVEL = 4 }
			add_restoration_perk_effect = { LEVEL = 5 }
		}
		effect = {
			add_trait = lifespan_magic_3
			add_character_flag = artificial_lifespan
			add_character_flag = natural_lifespan_0
		}
	}
	3355.1.1 = { give_nickname = nick_the_ageless }
	3360.1.1 = {
		effect = {
			add_arcana_skill = { VALUE = 12 }
		}
	}
	3400.1.1 = { death = yes }
	
	portrait_override={
		portrait_modifier_overrides={
			custom_clothes=male_clothes_religious_mage
			custom_cloaks=male_furs_secular_fp1_nobility_02
			custom_legwear=male_legwear_secular_fp1_common_01
			custom_hair=male_hair_western_07
			custom_beards=male_beard_rtt_01
			custom_headgear=male_headgear_religious_mage_02
		}
	}
}
